Example Response
API Documentation

collect_mvp

collect_mvp is a project that encompasses payment API and disbursement API. Before you can utilise payment and disbursement API, you must register and login to retrieve the bearer token by using the login and register API. In REST API calls, include the URL to the API service for the environment:

Sandbox: https://stg-collect-disburse.lyte.vc/
Live: https://collect-disburse.lyte.vc/

POST Client Credential Authentication
{{base}}/oauth/token

This endpoint logs in the client.

We login with clientid and clientsecret to retrieve a JWT token that will be used for the rest of the routes.

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "grant_type":"client_credentials",
    "client_id":"6",
    "scope": "*",
    "client_secret": "ZF6XAu694nZZ4LexPPYgb1y6lj2Ygp3xQpubV562"
}
Example Request
  • Client Credential Authentication Success
                                                
POST /oauth/token
{
    "grant_type":"client_credentials",
    "client_id":"3",
    "scope": "*",
    "client_secret": "5l2uPLpBdC58zenE6bkJC4QmrPjd3n7vgJ4AwLg9D"
}
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
{
    "token_type": "Bearer",
    "expires_in": 1296000,
    "access_token": "eyJ0eXAiOiJKV1QiLCJhbGciOiJSUzI1NiJ9.eyJhdWQiOiIzIiwianRpIjoiZDVmZWNhMjJhYmVhNjJiM2ZmNWU3MjYxYThlNmIzOGQ3OTRhNWQ2MzE4ZmYyOWZlZTg3MjBlMDQzNzM1MzMwZTA0MzMxYzk4MzAwZTE4YjUiLCJpYXQiOjE2MzAwMzMxMjguNDI3ODQ4LCJuYmYiOjE2MzAwMzMxMjguNDI3ODUzLCJleHAiOjE2MzEzMjkxMjguNDEwODk0LCJzdWIiOiIiLCJzY29wZXMiOlsiKiJdfQ.eaY3QmSkcqnkpRZbdFNJzX5sIwYR369LDZiImfPBL5Qw3gPU30ya84jXt9UyrHf7OgjyHfOZArakTB1Y2jlJtCNDHhSf3OWk2fw1vnC3pwjoGEGObFTNRBrtcoKy8J_24TtmHlKgGLypMT26OzzmWuuatwVZ1zNp8sUtDocdmpY"

POST Post a payment
{{base}}/api/v1/client/payments/

To create a payment object with the following information.
{ 'freelancer_ref' = '1', 'payer_name' = 'John Tan', 'payer_email' = 'johntan18@gmail.com', 'invoice_ref' = '4304329', 'payment_type' = 'credit', 'currency' = 'SGD', 'payment_amount' = '30', 'payment_status' = 'paid' };

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
  "freelancer_o_auth_id": "oauthid",
  "payer_name":"John Tan",
  "payer_email": "johntan18@gmail.com",
  "payer_contact": "4304329",
  "payment_reference": "credit",
  "currency": "SGD",
  "payment_amount" : "30",
  "description": "paid",
  "payment_status": "paid",
  "vendor": "paid"
  "invoice_ref": "reference",
}
Example Request
  • Post a payment (unauthenticated)
  • Post a payment success
                                                
POST /api/v1/client/payments/
{
  "freelancer_ref": "1",
  "payer_name":"John Tan",
  "payer_email": "johntan18@gmail.com",
  "invoice_ref": "4304329",
  "payment_type": "credit",
  "currency": "SGD",
  "payment_amount" : "30",
  "payment_status": "paid"
}
Example Response
401 - Unauthorized 
                                                    
{
    "error": "401 Unauthenticated"
}

DELETE Delete a payment
{{base}}/api/v1/client/payments/2

Delete payment object where {id} is the id of the payment object.

Returns 204 No Content when successful.

Example Request
  • Delete a payment success
  • Delete a payment (unauthenticated)
                                                
DELETE /api/v1/client/payments/2
                                            
                                                
DELETE /api/v1/client/payments/2

{
    "error": "401 Unauthenticated"
}
PUT Put a payment
{{base}}/api/v1/client/payments/2

Update payment object which belongs to id with it’s parameters such as freelancer_ref, payer_name, payer_email, invoice_ref, payment_type, currency, payment_amount, payment_status.

In the example, we update the payment object with id of 3 (payer_name to susan2).

HEADERS

None

PARAMS

None

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "payment_type": "credit"
}
Example Request
  • Put a payment (unauthenticated)
  • Put a payment
  • Put a non-existing payment
                                                
PUT /api/v1/client/payments/5
{
    "payment_type": "susan2"
}
Example Response
401 - Unauthorized 
                                                    
{
    "error": "401 Unauthenticated"
}
                                                
                                                
PUT /api/v1/client/payments/5
{
    "payment_type": "credit"
}
Example Response

    "data": {
        "id": 5,
        "fees": "0.00",
        "freelancer_ref": "contract_a40255b1313a49f7937b8891597d458c",
        "description": null,
        "payer_name": null,
        "payer_email": null,
        "invoice_ref": "penloytels0_1332l2zszkllz3ll3l4l56ozlzlll",
        "payment_type": "credit",
        "currency": "SGD",
        "payment_amount": null,
        "payment_status": "paid",
        "created_at": "2021-08-23 09:13:14",
        "updated_at": "2021-08-27 08:44:01",

    }

POST Post a disbursement
{{base}}/api/v1/client/disbursements/

To create a disbursement object with the following information.

{
‘invoiceref’ = “324123”,
‘payeename’ = “John Tan”,
‘bankcode’ = “323”,
‘bankaccountholdername’ = “John Tan”,
‘bankaccountnumber’ = “3202”,
‘countrycode’ = “65”,
‘disbursementamount’ = “30”,
‘disbursement_status’ = “completed”,
};

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "invoice_ref":"324123",
    "payee_name":"john tan",
    "bank_code":"323",
    "bank_account_holder_name":"John Tan",
    "bank_account_number":"3202",
    "country_code":"65",
    "amount":"30",
    "disbursement_status":"completed"
}
Example Request
  • Post a disbursement success
                                                
POST /api/v1/client/disbursements/
{
    "invoice_ref":"324123",
    "payee_name":"john tan",
    "bank_code":"323",
    "bank_account_holder_name":"John Tan",
    "bank_account_number":"3202",
    "country_code":"65",
    "disbursement_amount":"30",
    "disbursement_status":"completed"
}
Example Response
201 - Created 
                                                    
{
    "data": {
        "invoice_ref": "324123",
        "payee_name": "john tan",
        "bank_code": "323",
        "bank_account_holder_name": "John Tan",
        "bank_account_number": "3202",
        "country_code": "65",
        "disbursement_amount": "30",
        "disbursement_status": "completed",
        "updated_at": "2021-08-19 23:18:43",
        "created_at": "2021-08-19 23:18:43",
        "id": 3
    }
}

PUT Put a disbursement
{{base}}/api/v1/client/disbursements/2

Update disbursement object which belongs to id with it’s parameters such as invoice_ref, payee_name, bank_code, bank_account_holder_name, bank_account_number, country_code, disbursement_amount, disbursement_status.

In the example, we update the disbursement object with id of 3 (invoice_ref to 34).

BODY raw
                                                  
                                                    
{
    "invoice_ref" : "34"
}
Example Request
  • Put a disbursement success
  • Put a disbursement (Non-existing payment)
  • Put a disbursement (unauthenticated)
                                                
PUT /api/v1/disbursements/1
{
    "invoice_ref" : "34"
}
Example Response
202 - Accepted 
                                                    
{
    "data": {
        "id": 1,
        "invoice_ref": "34",
        "payee_name": "john tan",
        "bank_code": "323",
        "bank_account_holder_name": "John Tan",
        "bank_account_number": "3202",
        "country_code": "65",
        "disbursement_amount": "30.00",
        "disbursement_status": "completed",
        "created_at": "2021-07-27 07:17:07",
        "updated_at": "2021-08-04 02:30:45",
        "deleted_at": null
    }
}
                                                
                                                
PUT /api/v1/client/disbursements/100
{
    "invoice_ref" : "34"
}
Example Response
404 - Not Found

GET Export disbursements
{{base}}/api/v1/client/disbursements/export

Export disbursement objects with following catogeries “ID”,”Payee”,”Bank Code”,”Bank Account Holder Name”,”Bank Account Number”,”Payout Amount”.

HEADERS

None

BODY raw
Example Request
  • Export disbursements success
  • Export disbursements (unauthenticated)
                                                
GET /api/v1/client/disbursements/export
Example Response
200 - OK 
                                                    
"ID","Payee","Bank Code","Bank Account Holder Name","Bank Account Number","Payout Amount"
"324123","john tan","323","John Tan","3202","30"
"324123","john tan","323","John Tan","3202","30"

                                                
                                                
GET /api/v1/client/disbursements/export

POST Update disbursement status
https://sandbox.xfers.io/api/v4/disbursements/{id}/tasks

This endpoint updates the disbursement status to complete.

BODY raw

  "data": {
    "attributes": {
      "action": "complete"
    }
  }

POST Post a payment
{{base}}/api/v1/payments

This endpoint post a payment in xfers and store the record in our database.

Returns the responses from xfers.
